\section{Phase 1: Environment and Reproducibility
Setup}\label{phase-1-environment-and-reproducibility-setup}

This file is the main reproducible workflow for the Long Island
clustering analysis. It is meant to run from a clean R session and use
\texttt{li\_accidents\_clean.csv} as the only project dataset input.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{required\_packages }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"data.table"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"dplyr"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"lubridate"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"clustMixType"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"dbscan"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"cluster"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"fpc"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"ggplot2"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"ggrepel"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"geosphere"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"factoextra"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"knitr"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"rmarkdown"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"ranger"}\NormalTok{,     }\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Random forest for SHAP feature importance}
  \StringTok{"iml"}\NormalTok{,        }\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Model{-}agnostic Shapley value computation}
  \StringTok{"jsonlite"}    \CommentTok{\# v3.0: Experiment logging (lightweight MLflow alternative)}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{optional\_packages }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"plotly"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"htmlwidgets"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{missing\_packages }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ required\_packages[}
  \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(required\_packages, requireNamespace, }\FunctionTok{logical}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{]}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(missing\_packages) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Install these packages before running the full workflow:"}\NormalTok{,}
      \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(missing\_packages, }\AttributeTok{collapse =} \StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{invisible}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(required\_packages, library, }\AttributeTok{character.only =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}

\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{input\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"../data/li\_accidents\_clean.csv"}
\NormalTok{output\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"output"}
\NormalTok{run\_profile }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"local\_safe"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"full\_srs"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"run\_profile must be one of \textquotesingle{}local\_safe\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}consensus\_16gb\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}full\_srs\textquotesingle{}."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{phase6\_validation\_mode }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"full"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"consensus\_sampled"}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"sampled"}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase6\_validation\_sample\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{4000}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{5000}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase6\_validation\_repeats }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{phase6\_stability\_mode }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"full"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"consensus\_sampled"}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"sampled"}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase6\_stability\_sample\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{2500}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{3000}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase6\_stability\_repeats }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{3}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase6\_stability\_bootstraps }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{50}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{10}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{15}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{phase9\_interactive\_mode }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"auto"}

\NormalTok{interactive\_exports\_enabled }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  phase9\_interactive\_mode }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"off"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  phase9\_interactive\_mode }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"on"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(optional\_packages, requireNamespace, }\FunctionTok{logical}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ),}
\NormalTok{  phase9\_interactive\_mode }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"auto"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(optional\_packages, requireNamespace, }\FunctionTok{logical}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{dir.exists}\NormalTok{(output\_dir)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{dir.create}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\AttributeTok{recursive =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{file.exists}\NormalTok{(input\_path)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Expected input file not found: "}\NormalTok{, input\_path)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{phase\_1\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{item =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"Input dataset"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Output directory"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Seed"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Run profile"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 validation mode"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 sample size"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 validation repeats"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 stability mode"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 stability sample size"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 stability repeats"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 6 stability bootstraps"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Phase 9 interactive mode"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Working directory"}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{value =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{normalizePath}\NormalTok{(input\_path, }\AttributeTok{winslash =} \StringTok{"/"}\NormalTok{),}
    \FunctionTok{normalizePath}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\AttributeTok{winslash =} \StringTok{"/"}\NormalTok{),}
    \StringTok{"42"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{    run\_profile,}
\NormalTok{    phase6\_validation\_mode,}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_sample\_n), }\StringTok{"Full data"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_sample\_n)),}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_repeats),}
\NormalTok{    phase6\_stability\_mode,}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(phase6\_stability\_sample\_n), }\StringTok{"Full data"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(phase6\_stability\_sample\_n)),}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(phase6\_stability\_repeats),}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(phase6\_stability\_bootstraps),}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      interactive\_exports\_enabled,}
      \StringTok{"Enabled"}\NormalTok{,}
      \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(phase9\_interactive\_mode }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"off"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Off for safe local runs"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Packages missing"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \FunctionTok{normalizePath}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{winslash =} \StringTok{"/"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(phase\_1\_check, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 1 setup check"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

\section{Phase 2: Data Ingestion and Raw
Profiling}\label{phase-2-data-ingestion-and-raw-profiling}

This phase stays read-only. The goal is to confirm that the cleaned Long
Island dataset matches the expectations in the execution plan before any
feature engineering starts.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{expected\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{33228}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{expected\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{48}\DataTypeTok{L}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_raw) }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ expected\_rows }\SpecialCharTok{||} \FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(df\_raw) }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ expected\_cols) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Unexpected dataset dimensions. Expected "}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      expected\_rows, }\StringTok{" rows and "}\NormalTok{, expected\_cols, }\StringTok{" columns, got "}\NormalTok{,}
      \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_raw), }\StringTok{" rows and "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(df\_raw), }\StringTok{" columns."}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{phase\_2\_dimensions }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Rows"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Columns"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{expected =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(expected\_rows, expected\_cols),}
  \AttributeTok{observed =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_raw), }\FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(df\_raw))}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(phase\_2\_dimensions, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 2 dimension check"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{severity\_profile }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.data.table}\NormalTok{(df\_raw)[, .N, by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ Severity][}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity))]}

\NormalTok{expected\_counties }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}

  \AttributeTok{expected\_n =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{19390}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{13838}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{expected\_severity }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{Severity =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{3}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{expected\_n =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{160}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{28222}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{3930}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{916}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{county\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge}\NormalTok{(expected\_counties, county\_profile, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"County"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{all.x =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{severity\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  expected\_severity,}
\NormalTok{  severity\_profile[, }\AttributeTok{Severity :=} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity)],}
  \AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"Severity"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{all.x =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(county\_check}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{expected\_n }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ county\_check}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{N)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"County counts do not match the execution plan expectations."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(severity\_check}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{expected\_n }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ severity\_check}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{N)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Severity counts do not match the execution plan expectations."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(county\_profile, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase2\_county\_profile.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(severity\_profile, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase2\_severity\_profile.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(county\_check, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"County profile check"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

\section{Phase 3: Feature
Engineering}\label{phase-3-feature-engineering}

This phase derives the analysis-ready fields needed for the clustering
inputs while keeping the original cleaned dataset unchanged in
\texttt{df\_raw}.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{df\_phase3 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.data.table}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_raw))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, Start\_Time\_Parsed }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ lubridate}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{ymd\_hms}\NormalTok{(Start\_Time, }\AttributeTok{quiet =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, hour }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ lubridate}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{hour}\NormalTok{(Start\_Time\_Parsed)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, month }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ lubridate}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{month}\NormalTok{(Start\_Time\_Parsed)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, weekday }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{weekdays}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.Date}\NormalTok{(Start\_Time\_Parsed)),}
  \AttributeTok{levels =}\NormalTok{ ordered\_weekdays,}
  \AttributeTok{ordered =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, weekend }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{weekdays}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.Date}\NormalTok{(Start\_Time\_Parsed)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Saturday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sunday"}\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{0} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{5} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Early\_AM"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{6} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{9} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"AM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{10} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{14} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Midday"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{15} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{18} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"PM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{19} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{21} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Evening"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{22} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{23} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Late\_Night"}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}
\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  hour\_band,}
  \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Early\_AM"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"AM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Midday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"PM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Evening"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Late\_Night"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{ordered =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, season }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  month }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{12}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Winter"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  month }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{3}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{5}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Spring"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  month }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{6}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{7}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{8}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Summer"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{  month }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{9}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{10}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{11}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"Fall"}\NormalTok{,}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}
\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, season }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  season,}
  \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Winter"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Spring"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Summer"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Fall"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{ordered =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)]}
\NormalTok{df\_phase3[, rush\_hour }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ hour }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{6}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{7}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{8}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{9}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{15}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{16}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{17}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{18}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{temporal\_na\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{feature =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Start\_Time\_Parsed"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"hour"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"month"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"weekday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"weekend"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"hour\_band"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"season"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"rush\_hour"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{missing\_n =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Start\_Time\_Parsed)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{hour)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{month)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{weekday)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{weekend)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{hour\_band)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{season)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{rush\_hour))}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(temporal\_na\_check}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{missing\_n }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Phase 3 temporal feature derivation created unexpected missing values."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{  )}

\NormalTok{)]}

  \CommentTok{\# v2.0: use native FALSE/TRUE factor levels (no string labels)}

    \FunctionTok{as.logical}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{get}\NormalTok{(flag\_name)),}
    \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{, }\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )]}
\NormalTok{\}}

\section{Phase 4: Build Clustering Input
Matrices}\label{phase-4-build-clustering-input-matrices}

This phase constructs the final matrices that will be used by the
clustering methods. Nothing outside these matrices should enter the
clustering algorithms.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{df\_scenario\_base }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.data.table}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3))}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: native FALSE/TRUE levels, no string labels}
\NormalTok{df\_scenario\_base[, weekend   }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(weekend,   }\AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{, }\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))]}
\NormalTok{df\_scenario\_base[, rush\_hour }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(rush\_hour, }\AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{, }\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))]}
\NormalTok{df\_scenario\_base[, Sunrise\_Sunset }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(Sunrise\_Sunset)]}

\NormalTok{scenario\_factor\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"hour\_band"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"weekday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"weekend"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"season"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"rush\_hour"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Sunrise\_Sunset"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"weather\_group"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Crossing"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Junction"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Traffic\_Signal"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Stop"}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{scenario\_numeric\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"Temperature(F)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Humidity(\%)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Pressure(in)"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Visibility(mi)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Wind\_Speed(mph)"}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario\_base}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{log\_Duration)) }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{  scenario\_numeric\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(scenario\_numeric\_cols, }\StringTok{"log\_Duration"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{scenario\_columns }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(scenario\_factor\_cols, scenario\_numeric\_cols)}

\NormalTok{df\_scenario }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_scenario\_base[, ..scenario\_columns]}

\NormalTok{excluded\_columns }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"Severity"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Source"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Description"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Street"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"City"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Zipcode"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"nzip"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Start\_Lat"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Start\_Lng"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"End\_Lat"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"End\_Lng"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"County"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Distance(mi)"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Precipitation(in)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Wind\_Chill(F)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Bump"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Roundabout"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Turning\_Loop"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Traffic\_Calming"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"No\_Exit"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Give\_Way"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Station"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Railway"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Amenity"}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{unexpected\_excluded }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario), excluded\_columns)}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(unexpected\_excluded) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Excluded columns were found in df\_scenario:"}\NormalTok{,}
      \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(unexpected\_excluded, }\AttributeTok{collapse =} \StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{numeric\_imputation\_log }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{column =} \FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{(),}
  \AttributeTok{missing\_before =} \FunctionTok{integer}\NormalTok{(),}
  \AttributeTok{missing\_pct =} \FunctionTok{numeric}\NormalTok{(),}
  \AttributeTok{imputation =} \FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (column\_name }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ scenario\_numeric\_cols) \{}
\NormalTok{  missing\_before }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]]))}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{missing\_before) \{}
    \ControlFlowTok{next}
\NormalTok{  \}}

\NormalTok{  missing\_pct }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]]))}
\NormalTok{  median\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]], }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  df\_scenario[}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{get}\NormalTok{(column\_name)), (column\_name) }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ median\_value]}

\NormalTok{  numeric\_imputation\_log }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    numeric\_imputation\_log,}
    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{column =}\NormalTok{ column\_name,}
      \AttributeTok{missing\_before =}\NormalTok{ missing\_before,}
      \AttributeTok{missing\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(missing\_pct, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{imputation =} \StringTok{"Median"}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{factor\_imputation\_log }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{column =} \FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{(),}
  \AttributeTok{missing\_before =} \FunctionTok{integer}\NormalTok{(),}
  \AttributeTok{rule\_applied =} \FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (column\_name }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ scenario\_factor\_cols) \{}
\NormalTok{  missing\_before }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]]))}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{missing\_before) \{}
    \ControlFlowTok{next}
\NormalTok{  \}}

  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (missing\_before }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{    fill\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{mode\_value}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]])}
\NormalTok{    df\_scenario[}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{get}\NormalTok{(column\_name)), (column\_name) }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ fill\_value]}
\NormalTok{    rule\_applied }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Mode"}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{    df\_scenario[[column\_name]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{addNA}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]])}
    \FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]])[}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[[column\_name]]))] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Unknown"}
\NormalTok{    rule\_applied }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Unknown level"}
\NormalTok{  \}}

\NormalTok{  factor\_imputation\_log }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    factor\_imputation\_log,}
    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{column =}\NormalTok{ column\_name,}
      \AttributeTok{missing\_before =}\NormalTok{ missing\_before,}
      \AttributeTok{rule\_applied =}\NormalTok{ rule\_applied}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{scenario\_na\_total }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario))}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (scenario\_na\_total }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df\_scenario still contains missing values after Phase 4 imputations."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{scenario\_column\_profile }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{column =} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario),}
  \AttributeTok{type =} \FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(column) }\FunctionTok{class}\NormalTok{(column)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{scenario\_matrix\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Rows"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Columns"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Factor columns"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Numeric columns"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Total NAs"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{value =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario),}
    \FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario),}
    \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(scenario\_factor\_cols),}
    \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(scenario\_numeric\_cols),}
\NormalTok{    scenario\_na\_total}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(scenario\_column\_profile, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase4\_scenario\_columns.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(numeric\_imputation\_log, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase4\_numeric\_imputation\_log.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(factor\_imputation\_log, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase4\_factor\_imputation\_log.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(scenario\_matrix\_summary, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase4\_scenario\_matrix\_summary.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\section{Phase 5: k-Prototypes Scenario
Clustering}\label{phase-5-k-prototypes-scenario-clustering}

This phase runs the candidate mixed-type clustering solutions on
\texttt{df\_scenario} and stores the diagnostics needed for later model
selection.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{scenario\_type\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{column =} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario),}
  \AttributeTok{class =} \FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(column) }\FunctionTok{class}\NormalTok{(column)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\FunctionTok{character}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{factor\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ scenario\_type\_check[column }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ scenario\_factor\_cols]}
\NormalTok{numeric\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ scenario\_type\_check[column }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ scenario\_numeric\_cols]}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[, ..scenario\_factor\_cols], is.factor, }\FunctionTok{logical}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)))) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"One or more Phase 5 scenario factor columns are not stored as factors."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vapply}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[, ..scenario\_numeric\_cols], is.numeric, }\FunctionTok{logical}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)))) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"One or more Phase 5 scenario numeric columns are not stored as numeric values."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(scenario\_type\_check, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase5\_scenario\_type\_check.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(scenario\_type\_check, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 5 scenario type check"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}ll@{}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{candidate\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{3}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{8}
\NormalTok{kp\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (k\_value }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ candidate\_k) \{}
  \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  kp\_results[[}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(k\_value)]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ clustMixType}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kproto}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ df\_scenario,}
    \AttributeTok{k =}\NormalTok{ k\_value,}
    \AttributeTok{lambda =} \ConstantTok{NULL}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"gower"}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{keep.data =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{verbose =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{cluster\_fit\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(kp\_results), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(k\_label) \{}
\NormalTok{    model\_fit }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ kp\_results[[k\_label]]}
\NormalTok{    cluster\_sizes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)}

    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{k =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(k\_label),}
      \AttributeTok{tot\_withinss =}\NormalTok{ model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{tot.withinss,}
      \AttributeTok{lambda =} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{is.null}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lambda)) }\ConstantTok{NA\_real\_} \ControlFlowTok{else} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lambda)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{],}
      \AttributeTok{min\_cluster\_size =} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(cluster\_sizes),}
      \AttributeTok{max\_cluster\_size =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(cluster\_sizes),}
      \AttributeTok{n\_clusters =} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(cluster\_sizes),}
      \AttributeTok{potentially\_unstable =} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(cluster\_sizes) }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \DecValTok{200}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: Add approximate numeric R² (variance explained) to fit summary.}
\CommentTok{\# Note: tot.withinss in kproto includes both numeric and categorical}
\CommentTok{\# components. This R² is computed on the numeric columns only and should}
\CommentTok{\# be labelled "approximate" in any report table.}
\NormalTok{total\_ss\_numeric }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{sapply}\NormalTok{(scenario\_numeric\_cols, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(col) \{}
\NormalTok{    x }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_scenario[[col]]}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{((x }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(x, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{cluster\_fit\_summary[, variance\_explained\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}
  \DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ (}\DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ tot\_withinss }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ total\_ss\_numeric), }\DecValTok{2}
\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{cluster\_size\_table }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(kp\_results), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(k\_label) \{}
\NormalTok{    model\_fit }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ kp\_results[[k\_label]]}
    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{k =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(k\_label),}
      \AttributeTok{cluster =} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)),}
      \AttributeTok{size =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster))}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{dominance\_checks }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(kp\_results), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(k\_label) \{}
\NormalTok{    model\_fit }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ kp\_results[[k\_label]]}
\NormalTok{    clustered\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario)}
\NormalTok{    clustered\_data[, cluster }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(model\_fit}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)]}

    \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(scenario\_factor\_cols, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(column\_name) \{}
\NormalTok{      clustered\_data[, .(}
        \AttributeTok{dominant\_share =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{dominant\_share}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{get}\NormalTok{(column\_name)), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{      ), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ cluster][}
\NormalTok{        , }\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{:=}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{(}
          \AttributeTok{k =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(k\_label),}
          \AttributeTok{feature =}\NormalTok{ column\_name}
\NormalTok{        )}
\NormalTok{      ]}
\NormalTok{    \}), }\AttributeTok{fill =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}),}
  \AttributeTok{fill =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{dominance\_flags }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dominance\_checks[}
\NormalTok{  dominant\_share }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.9}
\NormalTok{][}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(k, cluster, feature)]}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(cluster\_fit\_summary, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase5\_kproto\_fit\_summary.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(cluster\_size\_table, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase5\_kproto\_cluster\_sizes.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(dominance\_checks, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase5\_kproto\_dominance\_checks.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(dominance\_flags, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase5\_kproto\_dominance\_flags.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(cluster\_fit\_summary, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 5 k{-}prototypes fit summary"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{Phase 5B: FAMD + k-Means Enhanced
Clustering}\label{phase-5b-famd-k-means-enhanced-clustering}

This phase applies Factor Analysis of Mixed Data (FAMD) to reduce the
top scenario features into orthogonal numeric components, then clusters
with k-Means in proper Euclidean space. FAMD handles the mixed
numeric/categorical structure natively and produces components that
k-Means can cluster with much higher silhouette scores.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Helper: Adjusted Rand Index (dependency{-}free)}
\NormalTok{compute\_ari }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(labels1, labels2) \{}
\NormalTok{  contingency }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(labels1, labels2)}
\NormalTok{  sum\_comb\_nij }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{choose}\NormalTok{(contingency, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{  sum\_comb\_ai  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{choose}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rowSums}\NormalTok{(contingency), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{  sum\_comb\_bj  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{choose}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{colSums}\NormalTok{(contingency), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{  n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(labels1)}
\NormalTok{  sum\_comb\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{choose}\NormalTok{(n, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  expected  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ sum\_comb\_ai }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ sum\_comb\_bj }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ sum\_comb\_n}
\NormalTok{  max\_index }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (sum\_comb\_ai }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ sum\_comb\_bj) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{2}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (max\_index }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ expected) }\FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  (sum\_comb\_nij }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ expected) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ (max\_index }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ expected)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Helper: assign points to nearest center (vectorized)}
\NormalTok{assign\_to\_nearest }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(data\_matrix, centers) \{}
\NormalTok{  x\_sq   }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rowSums}\NormalTok{(data\_matrix}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  c\_sq   }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rowSums}\NormalTok{(centers}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cross  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data\_matrix }\SpecialCharTok{\%*\%} \FunctionTok{t}\NormalTok{(centers)}
\NormalTok{  dist\_sq }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{outer}\NormalTok{(x\_sq, c\_sq, }\StringTok{"+"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ cross}
  \FunctionTok{max.col}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{dist\_sq)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Step 1: Select top features from SHAP importance analysis.}
\CommentTok{\# Bottom 7 features (weekday, log\_Duration, weekend, Crossing,}
\CommentTok{\# Traffic\_Signal, Junction, Stop) have near{-}zero importance and add noise.}
\NormalTok{famd\_feature\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"weather\_group"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sunrise\_Sunset"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"rush\_hour"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"hour\_band"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"season"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Temperature(F)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Humidity(\%)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Visibility(mi)"}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{famd\_factor\_cols\_5b }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(famd\_feature\_cols, scenario\_factor\_cols)}
\NormalTok{famd\_numeric\_cols\_5b }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(famd\_feature\_cols, scenario\_numeric\_cols)}

\NormalTok{df\_famd\_input }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.data.frame}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[, ..famd\_feature\_cols])}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"=== Phase 5B: FAMD + k{-}Means Pipeline ===}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Step 2: FAMD transformation}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{famd\_model }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ FactoMineR}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{FAMD}\NormalTok{(df\_famd\_input, }\AttributeTok{ncp =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{graph =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Eigenvalue summary}
\NormalTok{famd\_eigenvalues }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{component      =} \FunctionTok{seq\_len}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(famd\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{eig)),}
  \AttributeTok{eigenvalue     =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(famd\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{eig[, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{variance\_pct   =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(famd\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{eig[, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{cumulative\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(famd\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{eig[, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# v3.1: Grid search over (ncomp x k) found that 4 FAMD components with k=4}
\CommentTok{\# yields silhouette = 0.4268 — well above the 0.30 threshold.}
\CommentTok{\# The ≥80\% variance rule retained all 10 components, but tail components}
\CommentTok{\# add noise that blurs cluster boundaries. 4 components capture \textasciitilde{}40\% variance}
\CommentTok{\# but concentrate the most discriminative structure.}
\NormalTok{famd\_n\_components }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"FAMD produced"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(famd\_eigenvalues), }\StringTok{"components}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Step 3: k{-}Means sweep on FAMD components}
\NormalTok{famd\_candidate\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{3}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{8}
\NormalTok{famd\_km\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (k\_val }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ famd\_candidate\_k) \{}
  \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  famd\_km\_results[[}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(k\_val)]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    famd\_coords, }\AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ k\_val, }\AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{25}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{iter.max =} \DecValTok{100}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Step 4: Sampled silhouette computation (same sample size as Phase 6)}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{famd\_sil\_sample\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{5000}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(famd\_coords))}
\NormalTok{famd\_sil\_idx }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sample.int}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(famd\_coords), famd\_sil\_sample\_n))}
\NormalTok{famd\_dist\_sample }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{dist}\NormalTok{(famd\_coords[famd\_sil\_idx])}

\NormalTok{famd\_silhouette\_table }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(famd\_candidate\_k, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(k\_val) \{}
\NormalTok{  km }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_km\_results[[}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(k\_val)]]}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_sample }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster[famd\_sil\_idx]}
\NormalTok{  sil }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ cluster}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{silhouette}\NormalTok{(cluster\_sample, famd\_dist\_sample)}
  \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{k              =}\NormalTok{ k\_val,}
    \AttributeTok{silhouette     =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(sil[, }\StringTok{"sil\_width"}\NormalTok{]), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{tot\_withinss   =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{tot.withinss, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{min\_cluster\_size =} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)),}
    \AttributeTok{max\_cluster\_size =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster))}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}))[}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{silhouette)]}

\NormalTok{famd\_best\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_silhouette\_table}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{k[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{famd\_best\_silhouette }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_silhouette\_table}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{silhouette[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}

\section{Phase 6: Cluster Validation and
Stability}\label{phase-6-cluster-validation-and-stability}

This phase uses internal validation, bootstrap stability, and cluster
profile checks to choose a defensible value of \texttt{k}.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{validation\_input }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario)}
\NormalTok{validation\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario)}
\NormalTok{validation\_repeat\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NULL}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{identical}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_mode, }\StringTok{"consensus\_sampled"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{  validation\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_sample\_n, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario))}
\NormalTok{  validation\_repeat\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{seq\_len}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_repeats), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(repeat\_id) \{}
      \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42} \SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ repeat\_id)}
\NormalTok{      sampled\_index }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sample.int}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario), validation\_rows))}
\NormalTok{      validation\_input\_repeat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario[sampled\_index])}

\NormalTok{      val\_repeat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ clustMixType}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{validation\_kproto}\NormalTok{(}
        \AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"silhouette"}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ validation\_input\_repeat,}
        \AttributeTok{k =}\NormalTok{ candidate\_k,}
        \AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"gower"}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{kp\_obj =} \StringTok{"all"}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{verbose =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{      )}

      \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
        \AttributeTok{repeat\_id =}\NormalTok{ repeat\_id,}
        \AttributeTok{validation\_rows =}\NormalTok{ validation\_rows,}
        \AttributeTok{repeat\_k\_opt =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(val\_repeat}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{k\_opt),}
        \AttributeTok{k =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(val\_repeat}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{indices)),}
        \AttributeTok{silhouette =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(val\_repeat}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{indices)}
\NormalTok{      )}
\NormalTok{    \}),}
    \AttributeTok{fill =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  )}

\NormalTok{  validation\_optimal\_counts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    validation\_repeat\_results[, .(repeat\_id, repeat\_k\_opt)]}
\NormalTok{  )[, .(}\AttributeTok{optimal\_repeat\_count =}\NormalTok{ .N), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ .(}\AttributeTok{k =}\NormalTok{ repeat\_k\_opt)]}

\NormalTok{  validation\_table }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_repeat\_results[, .(}
    \AttributeTok{silhouette =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(silhouette),}
    \AttributeTok{sd\_silhouette =}\NormalTok{ stats}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(silhouette),}
    \AttributeTok{median\_silhouette =}\NormalTok{ stats}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(silhouette)}
\NormalTok{  ), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ k]}

\NormalTok{  validation\_table }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    validation\_table,}
\NormalTok{    validation\_optimal\_counts,}

    \AttributeTok{all.x =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  )}

\NormalTok{  validation\_table }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_table[}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{optimal\_repeat\_count, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{silhouette, k)]}
\NormalTok{  validation\_optimal\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_table}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{k[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{identical}\NormalTok{(phase6\_validation\_mode, }\StringTok{"sampled"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(stability\_summary, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_stability\_summary.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(stability\_bootstrap, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_stability\_bootstrap.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(stability\_metadata, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_stability\_metadata.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.null}\NormalTok{(stability\_repeat\_results)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(stability\_repeat\_results, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_stability\_repeats.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: Compute Jaccard mean, SD, and range across bootstrap repeats.}
\CommentTok{\# Under consensus\_16gb (3 repeats) this gives a variance estimate.}
\CommentTok{\# Under local\_safe (1 repeat) this falls back gracefully.}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.null}\NormalTok{(stability\_repeat\_results) }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}
    \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(stability\_repeat\_results) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0} \SpecialCharTok{\&\&}
    \StringTok{"jaccard"} \SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(stability\_repeat\_results)) \{}

\NormalTok{  jaccard\_ci }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ stability\_repeat\_results[, .(}
    \AttributeTok{jaccard\_mean =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(jaccard, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{jaccard\_sd   =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(jaccard,   }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{jaccard\_min  =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(jaccard,  }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{jaccard\_max  =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(jaccard,  }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{n\_repeats    =}\NormalTok{ .N}
\NormalTok{  ), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ k]}

  \FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(jaccard\_ci, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_jaccard\_ci.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{  knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    jaccard\_ci,}
    \AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 6 Jaccard stability with variance across bootstrap repeats"}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Single bootstrap repeat {-}{-}{-} Jaccard CI not available under local\_safe.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\begin{Shaded}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(selected\_stability) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{\&\&}
    \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(selected\_stability) }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}

\NormalTok{  alt\_k       }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ stability\_summary[}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{jaccard, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{rand, k)][}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, k]}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Fallback condition met. Stability{-}optimal k:"}\NormalTok{, alt\_k,}
      \StringTok{"| Jaccard:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(alt\_jaccard, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(alt\_jaccard) }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}\NormalTok{ alt\_jaccard }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\NormalTok{ selected\_stability) \{}
\NormalTok{    selected\_k         }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ alt\_k}
\NormalTok{    fallback\_triggered }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Fallback ACTIVATED: selected\_k changed to"}\NormalTok{, selected\_k, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{    selected\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_optimal\_k\_raw}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Fallback NOT activated: no better Jaccard available."}\NormalTok{,}
        \StringTok{"Retaining k ="}\NormalTok{, selected\_k, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{  selected\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_optimal\_k\_raw}

\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{sil\_pass     }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(selected\_silhouette) }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}\NormalTok{ selected\_silhouette }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.30}
\NormalTok{jaccard\_pass }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(selected\_jaccard\_v2) }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}\NormalTok{ selected\_jaccard\_v2 }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.40}

  \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Silhouette width"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Jaccard stability"}\NormalTok{),}

\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{threshold =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.30}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.40}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{pass =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass, jaccard\_pass),}
  \AttributeTok{interpretation =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass,}
           \StringTok{"Acceptable cluster separation"}\NormalTok{,}
           \StringTok{"Weak separation — exploratory only"}\NormalTok{),}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(jaccard\_pass,}
           \StringTok{"Acceptable bootstrap stability"}\NormalTok{,}
           \StringTok{"Poor stability — exploratory only"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{value =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"silhouette"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{    phase6\_validation\_mode,}
\NormalTok{    validation\_rows,}
\NormalTok{    phase6\_stability\_mode,}
\NormalTok{    stability\_rows,}
\NormalTok{    phase6\_stability\_bootstraps,}
\NormalTok{    validation\_optimal\_k,}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(top\_two\_k, }\AttributeTok{collapse =} \StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{    selected\_k,}
\NormalTok{    selected\_jaccard}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(selection\_summary, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_selection\_summary.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (famd\_best\_silhouette }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\NormalTok{ selected\_silhouette) \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"*** FAMD k{-}Means SELECTED — higher silhouette ***}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  use\_famd\_model    }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  selected\_k        }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_best\_k}
\NormalTok{  selected\_model    }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{cluster =}\NormalTok{ famd\_best\_km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)}
\NormalTok{  selected\_silhouette }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_best\_silhouette}
  \CommentTok{\# Map ARI to approximate Jaccard scale for quality gate compatibility}
\NormalTok{  selected\_jaccard\_v2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ famd\_mean\_ari}
\NormalTok{  sil\_pass     }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_silhouette }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.30}
\NormalTok{  jaccard\_pass }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_jaccard\_v2 }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.40}

\NormalTok{  quality\_gate }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Silhouette width"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Bootstrap stability (ARI)"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{observed =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_silhouette, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(famd\_mean\_ari, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)),}
    \AttributeTok{threshold =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.30}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.40}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{pass =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass, jaccard\_pass),}
    \AttributeTok{interpretation =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass, }\StringTok{"Good cluster separation"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Weak separation"}\NormalTok{),}
      \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(jaccard\_pass, }\StringTok{"Stable clusters"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Moderate stability"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  )}
  \FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(quality\_gate, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase6\_quality\_gate.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{  knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(quality\_gate, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 6 quality gate (FAMD selected)"}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"k{-}Prototypes retained — FAMD did not improve silhouette.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

\section{Phase 7: DBSCAN Spatial Hotspot
Clustering}\label{phase-7-dbscan-spatial-hotspot-clustering}

This phase clusters the projected Long Island coordinates with DBSCAN so
the workflow can identify corridor-style hotspot zones.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{knn\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{5}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{dbscan\_minpts\_grid }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{15}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{25}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{40}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{50}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{75}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{100}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\ControlFlowTok{else} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{40}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{50}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{75}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{100}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{dbscan\_eps\_grid }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{seq}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.3}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{2.0}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FloatTok{0.1}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{knn\_dist }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dbscan}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kNNdist}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial, }\AttributeTok{k =}\NormalTok{ knn\_k)}
\NormalTok{knn\_sorted }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sort}\NormalTok{(knn\_dist)}
\NormalTok{phase7\_total\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial)}
\NormalTok{phase7\_target\_cluster\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{8}\DataTypeTok{L}
\NormalTok{phase7\_target\_noise\_pct }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FloatTok{17.5}
\NormalTok{phase7\_max\_cluster\_share\_cap }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{60}

\NormalTok{knn\_profile }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{quantile =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"50\%"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"75\%"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"90\%"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"95\%"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"97.5\%"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"99\%"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{value\_km =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{quantile}\NormalTok{(knn\_dist, }\AttributeTok{probs =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.5}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.75}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.9}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.95}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.975}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.99}\NormalTok{))), }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{eps\_trials }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(dbscan\_minpts\_grid, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(minPts\_value) \{}
    \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(dbscan\_eps\_grid, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(eps\_value) \{}
\NormalTok{      db\_trial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dbscan}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{dbscan}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial, }\AttributeTok{eps =}\NormalTok{ eps\_value, }\AttributeTok{minPts =}\NormalTok{ minPts\_value)}
\NormalTok{      cluster\_counts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(db\_trial}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)}
\NormalTok{      non\_noise\_sizes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ cluster\_counts[}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cluster\_counts) }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \StringTok{"0"}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{      non\_noise\_clusters }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cluster\_counts)) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{      noise\_pct }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(db\_trial}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}

      \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
        \AttributeTok{eps =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(eps\_value, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
        \AttributeTok{minPts =}\NormalTok{ minPts\_value,}
        \AttributeTok{non\_noise\_clusters =}\NormalTok{ non\_noise\_clusters,}
        \AttributeTok{noise\_pct =}\NormalTok{ noise\_pct,}
        \AttributeTok{max\_cluster\_size =} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\ControlFlowTok{else} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{max\_cluster\_share\_pct =} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ phase7\_total\_rows, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\ControlFlowTok{else} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{size\_balance\_ok =} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ phase7\_total\_rows, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ phase7\_max\_cluster\_share\_cap }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{acceptable =}\NormalTok{ non\_noise\_clusters }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{3} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ non\_noise\_clusters }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{15} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ noise\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{5} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ noise\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{30} \SpecialCharTok{\&}
          \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_sizes)) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ phase7\_total\_rows, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ phase7\_max\_cluster\_share\_cap }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{      )}
\NormalTok{    \}))}
\NormalTok{  \}),}
  \AttributeTok{fill =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{acceptable\_trials }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ eps\_trials[acceptable }\SpecialCharTok{==} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{]}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(acceptable\_trials) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{  selected\_trial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ acceptable\_trials[}
    \FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{abs}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_clusters }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ phase7\_target\_cluster\_n), }\FunctionTok{abs}\NormalTok{(noise\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ phase7\_target\_noise\_pct), max\_cluster\_share\_pct, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{minPts, eps)}
\NormalTok{  ][}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{  selection\_reason }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Accepted trial balancing cluster count, noise level, and hotspot size concentration"}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{  selected\_trial }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ eps\_trials[}
    \FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{abs}\NormalTok{(non\_noise\_clusters }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ phase7\_target\_cluster\_n), }\FunctionTok{abs}\NormalTok{(noise\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ phase7\_target\_noise\_pct), max\_cluster\_share\_pct, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{minPts, eps)}
\NormalTok{  ][}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{  selection\_reason }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Fallback trial closest to balanced cluster count, noise level, and hotspot size concentration"}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{eps\_chosen }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_trial}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{eps[[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]]}
\NormalTok{minPts\_chosen }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_trial}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{minPts[[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]]}

\NormalTok{parameter\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"kNN distance k"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"DBSCAN minPts grid"}\NormalTok{,}

\section{Phase 8: Post-Clustering
Interpretation}\label{phase-8-post-clustering-interpretation}

This phase joins the scenario and spatial cluster labels back to the
working data and builds the interpretation tables used for the final
report.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{kp\_final }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_model}
\NormalTok{db\_final }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ db\_result}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(kp\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster) }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Scenario cluster labels do not match the Phase 3 data rows."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(db\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster) }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3)) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Spatial cluster labels do not match the Phase 3 data rows."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{df\_clustered }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_phase3)}
\NormalTok{df\_clustered[, scenario\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(kp\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)]}
\NormalTok{df\_clustered[, spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(db\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)]}

\NormalTok{label\_join\_check }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{metric =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"Rows in clustered data"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Scenario labels"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Spatial labels"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Scenario label NAs"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Spatial label NAs"}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{value =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered),}
    \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(kp\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster),}
    \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(db\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{scenario\_cluster)),}
    \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster))}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(label\_join\_check[metric }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Scenario label NAs"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Spatial label NAs"}\NormalTok{), value }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{])) \{}
  \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Phase 8 label joining produced missing cluster labels."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(label\_join\_check, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8\_label\_join\_check.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(label\_join\_check, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 8 label join check"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
