\NormalTok{scenario\_severity\_profile }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_clustered[, .(}
  \AttributeTok{n =}\NormalTok{ .N,}
  \AttributeTok{sev1\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev2\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev3\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev4\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev34\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ scenario\_cluster][}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(scenario\_cluster)]}

\NormalTok{scenario\_severity\_profile[, high\_risk\_archetype }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ (}
\NormalTok{  sev4\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ (}\FloatTok{1.5} \SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev4\_pct) }\SpecialCharTok{|}
\NormalTok{    sev34\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{==} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(sev34\_pct)}
\NormalTok{)]}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: Add explicit Sev4 rate and ratio{-}to{-}baseline columns}
\NormalTok{scenario\_severity\_profile[, sev4\_rate       }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ sev4\_pct]}
\NormalTok{scenario\_severity\_profile[, sev4\_vs\_baseline }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(sev4\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev4\_pct, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)]}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: Prepend a baseline row (scenario\_cluster = 0) for easy comparison}
\NormalTok{baseline\_severity\_row }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{scenario\_cluster =} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{n                =} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered),}
  \AttributeTok{sev1\_pct         =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev2\_pct         =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev3\_pct         =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(df\_clustered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Severity) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{sev4\_pct         =}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev4\_pct,}
  \AttributeTok{sev34\_pct        =}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev34\_pct,}
  \AttributeTok{high\_risk\_archetype =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{sev4\_rate        =}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev4\_pct,}
  \AttributeTok{sev4\_vs\_baseline =} \FloatTok{1.00}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{severity\_profile\_v2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(baseline\_severity\_row, scenario\_severity\_profile, }\AttributeTok{fill =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(severity\_profile\_v2, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8\_severity\_profile\_v2.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(scenario\_severity\_profile, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8\_scenario\_severity\_profile.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{spatial\_scenario\_crosstab }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_clustered[spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, .N, by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ .(spatial\_cluster, scenario\_cluster)][}
  \FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(spatial\_cluster, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{N, scenario\_cluster)}
\NormalTok{][}
\NormalTok{  , spatial\_cluster\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ N }\SpecialCharTok{/} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(N), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ spatial\_cluster}
\NormalTok{]}

\NormalTok{spatial\_scenario\_crosstab }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  spatial\_scenario\_crosstab,}
\NormalTok{  non\_noise\_assignments[, .(spatial\_cluster, corridor\_label)],}
  \AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"spatial\_cluster"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{all.x =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{spatial\_scenario\_crosstab }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  spatial\_scenario\_crosstab,}
\NormalTok{  scenario\_name\_lookup,}
  \AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"scenario\_cluster"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{all.x =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{spatial\_scenario\_dominance }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ spatial\_scenario\_crosstab[}
  \FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(spatial\_cluster, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{N, scenario\_cluster)}
\NormalTok{][}
\NormalTok{  , .SD[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ spatial\_cluster}
\NormalTok{][}
\NormalTok{  , .(}
\NormalTok{    spatial\_cluster,}
\NormalTok{    corridor\_label,}
    \AttributeTok{dominant\_scenario\_cluster =}\NormalTok{ scenario\_cluster,}
    \AttributeTok{dominant\_scenario\_name =}\NormalTok{ working\_name,}
    \AttributeTok{dominant\_count =}\NormalTok{ N,}
    \AttributeTok{dominant\_pct =}\NormalTok{ spatial\_cluster\_pct}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{]}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(spatial\_scenario\_crosstab, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8\_spatial\_scenario\_crosstab.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(spatial\_scenario\_dominance, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8\_spatial\_scenario\_dominance.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\end{Highlighting}

\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{scenario\_final\_names[, final\_name }\SpecialCharTok{:=}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
  \CommentTok{\# Tier 1: Extreme weather}
\NormalTok{  dominant\_weather\_group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Snow\_Ice"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \StringTok{"Winter Adverse {-}{-}{-} Snow and Ice"}\NormalTok{,}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 2: Night + hazardous visibility}
\NormalTok{  night\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{50} \SpecialCharTok{\&}
\NormalTok{    dominant\_weather\_group }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Fog\_Haze"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Rain"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Thunderstorm"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \StringTok{"Night Low{-}Visibility {-}{-}{-} Fog and Rain"}\NormalTok{,}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 3: Night / early morning (any weather)}
\NormalTok{  night\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{50} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ dominant\_hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Early\_AM"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Night / Early AM {-}{-}{-}"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_weather\_group)),}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 4: Weekend surface road}
\NormalTok{  weekend\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{40} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ traffic\_signal\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{8} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \StringTok{"Weekend Surface Road {-}{-}{-} Signal Heavy"}\NormalTok{,}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 5: Rush{-}hour corridor}
\NormalTok{  dominant\_hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"AM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"PM\_Rush"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ junction\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{10} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_weather\_group),}
      \FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_hour\_band),}
      \StringTok{"{-}{-}{-} Junction Heavy"}
\NormalTok{    ),}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 6 (v2.0): Cloudy off{-}peak daytime — captures generic midday clusters}
\NormalTok{  dominant\_weather\_group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Cloudy"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}
\NormalTok{    dominant\_hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Midday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Evening"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cloudy Off{-}Peak {-}{-}{-}"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_hour\_band)),}

  \CommentTok{\# Tier 7 (v2.0): Clear off{-}peak daytime}
\NormalTok{  dominant\_weather\_group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Clear"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}
\NormalTok{    dominant\_hour\_band }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Midday"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Evening"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Clear Off{-}Peak {-}{-}{-}"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_hour\_band)),}

  \CommentTok{\# Fallback: more informative than bare cluster number}
  \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}
    \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Mixed Conditions {-}{-}{-}"}\NormalTok{,}
      \FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_weather\_group),}
      \FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{, dominant\_hour\_band)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{scenario\_final\_names[, final\_name }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  high\_risk\_archetype,}
  \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(final\_name, }\StringTok{"(High Risk)"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  final\_name}
\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{duplicate\_scenario\_names }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ scenario\_final\_names[, .N, by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ final\_name][N }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, final\_name]}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(duplicate\_scenario\_names) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}

\NormalTok{\}}

\section{Phase 8B: SHAP Cluster Explanation
(v3.0)}\label{phase-8b-shap-cluster-explanation-v3.0}

This phase bridges the unsupervised and supervised worlds. We train a
Random Forest to predict cluster membership using the scenario features,
then compute Shapley values to explain \emph{which features drive each
cluster's identity}. This is a published technique called ``post-hoc
cluster explanation'' --- it does not replace the unsupervised
clustering, but adds interpretive depth.

\textbf{Why this matters:} Phase 8 tells us \emph{what} each cluster
looks like (e.g., ``74.8\% nighttime''). Phase 8B tells us \emph{how
much each feature contributes} to separating that cluster from the
others.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Build a supervised classifier on the unsupervised cluster labels.}
\CommentTok{\# This is NOT a predictive model — it\textquotesingle{}s an interpretation tool.}
\CommentTok{\# We use the same df\_scenario features that went into k{-}prototypes.}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"=== Phase 8B: SHAP Cluster Explanation (v3.0) ===}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## === Phase 8B: SHAP Cluster Explanation (v3.0) ===
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Prepare the training data: scenario features + cluster label as target}
\NormalTok{shap\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(df\_scenario)}

\CommentTok{\# Convert all factors to character then back to factor to ensure clean levels}
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (col\_name }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ scenario\_factor\_cols) \{}
\NormalTok{  shap\_data[[col\_name]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(shap\_data[[col\_name]]))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Sanitize column names — ranger\textquotesingle{}s formula interface rejects names with (), \%, etc.}
\NormalTok{old\_names }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(shap\_data)}
\NormalTok{new\_names }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{make.names}\NormalTok{(old\_names, }\AttributeTok{unique =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{setnames}\NormalTok{(shap\_data, old\_names, new\_names)}
\NormalTok{shap\_name\_map }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{setNames}\NormalTok{(old\_names, new\_names)  }\CommentTok{\# for restoring labels later}

\NormalTok{shap\_data[, cluster\_label }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C"}\NormalTok{, kp\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster),}
  \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(kp\_final}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)))}
\NormalTok{)]}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Training data dimensions:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(shap\_data), }\StringTok{"x"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(shap\_data), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\end{verbatim}

  \AttributeTok{formula         =}\NormalTok{ cluster\_label }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ .,}
  \AttributeTok{data            =}\NormalTok{ shap\_data,}
  \AttributeTok{num.trees       =} \DecValTok{500}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{importance      =} \StringTok{"permutation"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{probability     =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{min.node.size   =} \DecValTok{20}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{seed            =} \DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{num.threads     =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{detectCores}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{Random Forest OOB error:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{prediction.error, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Compute Shapley values on a representative subsample.}
\CommentTok{\# Full Shapley is expensive (model{-}agnostic), so we use 500 rows.}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{shap\_sample\_n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{500}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(shap\_data))}
\NormalTok{shap\_sample\_idx }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sample.int}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(shap\_data), shap\_sample\_n))}

\NormalTok{shap\_features }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ shap\_data[shap\_sample\_idx, }\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"cluster\_label"}\NormalTok{), with }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{shap\_target   }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ shap\_data[shap\_sample\_idx, cluster\_label]}

\CommentTok{\# Create iml Predictor object}
\CommentTok{\# Note: use a custom predict function because iml passes type="prob" to}
\CommentTok{\# ranger, but ranger only accepts type="response" (which already returns}
\CommentTok{\# probabilities when the model was trained with probability=TRUE).}
\NormalTok{predictor\_obj }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ iml}\SpecialCharTok{::}\NormalTok{Predictor}\SpecialCharTok{$}\FunctionTok{new}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{model =}\NormalTok{ rf\_cluster\_model,}
  \AttributeTok{data  =} \FunctionTok{as.data.frame}\NormalTok{(shap\_features),}
  \AttributeTok{y     =}\NormalTok{ shap\_target,}
  \AttributeTok{predict.function =} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(model, newdata) \{}
    \FunctionTok{predict}\NormalTok{(model, }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ newdata, }\AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"response"}\NormalTok{)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{predictions}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Computing Shapley values for"}\NormalTok{, shap\_sample\_n, }\StringTok{"observations...}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## Computing Shapley values for 500 observations...
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"This may take 2{-}5 minutes depending on hardware.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## This may take 2-5 minutes depending on hardware.

\NormalTok{  predictor\_obj,}
  \AttributeTok{loss   =} \StringTok{"ce"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{n.repetitions =} \DecValTok{5}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  , .(}
    \AttributeTok{feature           =}\NormalTok{ feature,}
    \AttributeTok{importance\_mean   =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(importance, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{importance\_sd     =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(importance}\FloatTok{.05}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}

\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{][}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{importance\_mean)]}

\NormalTok{  shap\_feature\_effects\_table,}

\NormalTok{)}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Per{-}cluster feature importance via one{-}vs{-}rest RF importance.}
\CommentTok{\# This tells us which features drive EACH specific cluster.}
\NormalTok{cluster\_specific\_importance }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbindlist}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label),}
  \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(target\_cluster) \{}
\NormalTok{    shap\_data\_ovr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{copy}\NormalTok{(shap\_data)}
\NormalTok{    shap\_data\_ovr[, target }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(cluster\_label }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ target\_cluster, }\StringTok{"target"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"other"}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"other"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"target"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )]}
\NormalTok{    shap\_data\_ovr[, cluster\_label }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \ConstantTok{NULL}\NormalTok{]}

    \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    rf\_ovr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ranger}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{ranger}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{formula       =}\NormalTok{ target }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ .,}
      \AttributeTok{data          =}\NormalTok{ shap\_data\_ovr,}
      \AttributeTok{num.trees     =} \DecValTok{300}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{importance    =} \StringTok{"permutation"}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{probability   =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{min.node.size =} \DecValTok{20}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{seed          =} \DecValTok{42}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{num.threads   =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{detectCores}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}

\NormalTok{    imp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ranger}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{importance}\NormalTok{(rf\_ovr)}
    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{cluster    =}\NormalTok{ target\_cluster,}
      \AttributeTok{feature    =} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(imp),}
      \AttributeTok{importance =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(imp)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Restore original column names for display}
\NormalTok{cluster\_specific\_importance[, feature }\SpecialCharTok{:=} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  feature }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(shap\_name\_map),}
\NormalTok{  shap\_name\_map[feature],}
\NormalTok{  feature}
\NormalTok{)]}

\CommentTok{\# Identify top 8 features per cluster}
\NormalTok{cluster\_top\_features }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ cluster\_specific\_importance[}
\NormalTok{  , .SD[}\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{importance)][}\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(.N, }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{)],}
\NormalTok{  by }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ cluster}
\NormalTok{]}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_specific\_importance,}
  \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8b\_cluster\_specific\_importance.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Create faceted importance plot by cluster}
\NormalTok{cluster\_importance\_plot }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_top\_features,}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{x    =}\NormalTok{ stats}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{reorder}\NormalTok{(feature, importance),}
    \AttributeTok{y    =}\NormalTok{ importance,}
    \AttributeTok{fill =}\NormalTok{ cluster}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{geom\_col}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{width =} \FloatTok{0.7}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{show.legend =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{coord\_flip}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{facet\_wrap}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ cluster, }\AttributeTok{scales =} \StringTok{"free\_y"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{ncol =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{scale\_fill\_brewer}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{palette =} \StringTok{"Set2"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{title    =} \StringTok{"Phase 8B: Feature Importance by Cluster (One{-}vs{-}Rest)"}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{subtitle =} \StringTok{"Top 8 features driving each cluster\textquotesingle{}s identity"}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{x        =} \ConstantTok{NULL}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{y        =} \StringTok{"Permutation importance"}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{theme\_bw}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{base\_size =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{  ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{theme}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{plot.title       =}\NormalTok{ ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{element\_text}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{face =} \StringTok{"bold"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{strip.text       =}\NormalTok{ ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{element\_text}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{face =} \StringTok{"bold"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{panel.grid.minor =}\NormalTok{ ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{element\_blank}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{  )}

\FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(cluster\_importance\_plot)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\pandocbounded{\includegraphics[keepaspectratio]{/Users/survaghasiya/Documents/AMS 597 Statistical computing Project/Longisland_Clustering/output/li_clustering_v3_files/figure-latex/phase-8b-cluster-specific-importance-1.pdf}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ggplot2}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{ggsave}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{filename =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8b\_cluster\_specific\_importance.png"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{plot     =}\NormalTok{ cluster\_importance\_plot,}
  \AttributeTok{width    =} \DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{height   =} \FloatTok{2.5} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label)) }\SpecialCharTok{+} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{dpi      =} \DecValTok{300}
\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Classification accuracy table — how well can a RF recover each cluster?}
\CommentTok{\# High accuracy = cluster is well{-}separated on these features.}
\CommentTok{\# Low accuracy = cluster overlaps with others (consistent with low silhouette).}
\NormalTok{rf\_predictions }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{predictions}
\NormalTok{rf\_predicted\_class }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(rf\_predictions)[}\FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(rf\_predictions, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, which.max)],}
  \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label)}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{confusion\_raw }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{Actual    =}\NormalTok{ shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label,}
  \AttributeTok{Predicted =}\NormalTok{ rf\_predicted\_class}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{cluster\_accuracy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{cluster =} \FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label),}
  \AttributeTok{n       =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label)),}
  \AttributeTok{correct =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{diag}\NormalTok{(confusion\_raw)),}
  \AttributeTok{accuracy\_pct =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{diag}\NormalTok{(confusion\_raw) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(shap\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster\_label), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{cluster\_accuracy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_accuracy,}
  \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{cluster =} \StringTok{"Overall"}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{n =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(cluster\_accuracy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{n),}
    \AttributeTok{correct =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(cluster\_accuracy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{correct),}
    \AttributeTok{accuracy\_pct =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(cluster\_accuracy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{correct) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(cluster\_accuracy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{n), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(cluster\_accuracy, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8b\_cluster\_accuracy.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_accuracy,}
  \AttributeTok{caption =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"Phase 8B cluster classification accuracy. "}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"OOB error = "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{prediction.error, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{". "}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"High accuracy = well{-}separated cluster. Low accuracy = fuzzy boundaries."}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

\section{Phase 8C: Experiment Logging
(v3.0)}\label{phase-8c-experiment-logging-v3.0}

This phase provides structured, reproducible logging of all clustering
parameters, quality metrics, and outputs --- serving the same purpose as
MLflow experiment tracking, but implemented natively in R without
requiring a Python backend or server infrastructure.

Every run of this workflow generates a timestamped JSON experiment
record that can be compared across runs (different profiles, feature
sets, or k values) to track how changes affect quality metrics.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# v3.0: Lightweight experiment tracking — replaces MLflow for academic workflows.}
\CommentTok{\# Captures all parameters, metrics, and artifact paths in a single JSON record.}

\NormalTok{experiment\_record }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{experiment\_id   =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"li\_clustering\_"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{format}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.time}\NormalTok{(), }\StringTok{"\%Y\%m\%d\_\%H\%M\%S"}\NormalTok{)),}
  \AttributeTok{timestamp       =} \FunctionTok{format}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.time}\NormalTok{(), }\StringTok{"\%Y{-}\%m{-}\%dT\%H:\%M:\%S\%z"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{workflow\_version =} \StringTok{"v3.0"}\NormalTok{,}

  \CommentTok{\# Run configuration}
  \AttributeTok{parameters =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{run\_profile            =}\NormalTok{ run\_profile,}
    \AttributeTok{random\_seed            =} \DecValTok{42}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{input\_file             =} \FunctionTok{normalizePath}\NormalTok{(input\_path, }\AttributeTok{winslash =} \StringTok{"/"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{total\_rows             =} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_raw),}
    \AttributeTok{total\_columns          =} \FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(df\_raw),}
    \AttributeTok{scenario\_features      =}\NormalTok{ scenario\_columns,}
    \AttributeTok{reduced\_features       =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(scenario\_factor\_cols, reduced\_numeric\_cols),}
    \AttributeTok{candidate\_k\_range      =} \FunctionTok{as.list}\NormalTok{(candidate\_k),}
    \AttributeTok{selected\_k             =}\NormalTok{ selected\_k,}
    \AttributeTok{dbscan\_eps             =}\NormalTok{ eps\_chosen,}
    \AttributeTok{dbscan\_minpts          =}\NormalTok{ minPts\_chosen,}
    \AttributeTok{validation\_mode        =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_validation\_mode,}
    \AttributeTok{validation\_sample\_n    =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_validation\_sample\_n,}
    \AttributeTok{validation\_repeats     =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_validation\_repeats,}
    \AttributeTok{stability\_mode         =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_stability\_mode,}
    \AttributeTok{stability\_sample\_n     =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_stability\_sample\_n,}
    \AttributeTok{stability\_repeats      =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_stability\_repeats,}
    \AttributeTok{stability\_bootstraps   =}\NormalTok{ phase6\_stability\_bootstraps}
\NormalTok{  ),}

  \CommentTok{\# Quality metrics}
  \AttributeTok{metrics =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{scenario\_clustering =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{selected\_k         =}\NormalTok{ selected\_k,}
      \AttributeTok{silhouette         =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_silhouette, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{silhouette\_pass    =}\NormalTok{ sil\_pass,}
      \AttributeTok{jaccard            =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_jaccard\_v2, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{jaccard\_pass       =}\NormalTok{ jaccard\_pass,}
      \AttributeTok{quality\_verdict    =} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}\NormalTok{ jaccard\_pass, }\StringTok{"ACCEPTABLE"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"EXPLORATORY"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{spatial\_clustering =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{non\_noise\_clusters      =} \FunctionTok{uniqueN}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster[df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{]),}
      \AttributeTok{noise\_pct               =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{largest\_cluster\_share   =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(largest\_non\_noise\_share\_pct, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{all\_srs\_targets\_met     =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{shap\_explanation =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{rf\_oob\_error           =} \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{prediction.error, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{rf\_num\_trees           =}\NormalTok{ rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{num.trees,}
      \AttributeTok{shap\_sample\_n          =}\NormalTok{ shap\_sample\_n,}
      \AttributeTok{top\_3\_features         =}\NormalTok{ shap\_global\_importance[}\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, feature]}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{severity\_findings =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{dataset\_sev4\_baseline  =}\NormalTok{ dataset\_sev4\_pct,}
      \AttributeTok{high\_risk\_clusters     =}\NormalTok{ scenario\_severity\_profile[high\_risk\_archetype }\SpecialCharTok{==} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, scenario\_cluster],}
      \AttributeTok{max\_sev4\_multiplier    =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(scenario\_severity\_profile}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{sev4\_vs\_baseline)}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ),}

  \CommentTok{\# Output artifact paths}
  \AttributeTok{artifacts =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{clustered\_dataset      =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"li\_accidents\_clustered.csv"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{figure\_directory       =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"figures"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{table\_directory        =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"tables"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{shap\_importance\_plot   =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8b\_global\_importance.png"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{shap\_cluster\_plot      =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8b\_cluster\_specific\_importance.png"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{experiment\_log         =} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8c\_experiment\_log.json"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ),}

  \CommentTok{\# Environment}
  \AttributeTok{environment =} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{r\_version      =} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(R.version}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{major, R.version}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{minor, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{platform       =}\NormalTok{ R.version}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{platform,}
    \AttributeTok{working\_dir    =} \FunctionTok{normalizePath}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{winslash =} \StringTok{"/"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{packages       =} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(required\_packages, }\AttributeTok{collapse =} \StringTok{", "}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Write as formatted JSON}
\NormalTok{experiment\_json }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ jsonlite}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{toJSON}\NormalTok{(experiment\_record, }\AttributeTok{pretty =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{auto\_unbox =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{writeLines}\NormalTok{(experiment\_json, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8c\_experiment\_log.json"}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Also create a flat summary CSV for quick scanning}
\NormalTok{experiment\_flat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{parameter =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"workflow\_version"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"run\_profile"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"selected\_k"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"silhouette"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sil\_pass"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"jaccard"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"jaccard\_pass"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"quality\_verdict"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"spatial\_clusters"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"noise\_pct"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"rf\_oob\_error"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"top\_feature\_1"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"top\_feature\_2"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"top\_feature\_3"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"dataset\_sev4\_baseline"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"max\_sev4\_multiplier"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"timestamp"}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{value =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"v3.0"}\NormalTok{, run\_profile, selected\_k,}
    \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_silhouette, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), sil\_pass,}
    \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_jaccard\_v2, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), jaccard\_pass,}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(sil\_pass }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&}\NormalTok{ jaccard\_pass, }\StringTok{"ACCEPTABLE"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"EXPLORATORY"}\NormalTok{),}
    \FunctionTok{uniqueN}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster[df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{]),}
    \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(df\_spatial\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{spatial\_cluster }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
    \FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(rf\_cluster\_model}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{prediction.error, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{    shap\_global\_importance[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, feature],}
\NormalTok{    shap\_global\_importance[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, feature],}
\NormalTok{    shap\_global\_importance[}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, feature],}
\NormalTok{    dataset\_sev4\_pct,}
    \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(scenario\_severity\_profile}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{sev4\_vs\_baseline),}
    \FunctionTok{format}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.time}\NormalTok{(), }\StringTok{"\%Y{-}\%m{-}\%dT\%H:\%M:\%S"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(experiment\_flat, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8c\_experiment\_summary.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Experiment log written to:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase8c\_experiment\_log.json"}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{Phase 9: Export and
Visualization}\label{phase-9-export-and-visualization}

This phase organizes the report-ready figures, tables, and labeled
dataset export so the final write-up can pull from a single output
location.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{figure\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"figures"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{table\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"tables"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{interactive\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"interactive"}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{dir.create}\NormalTok{(figure\_dir, }\AttributeTok{recursive =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{showWarnings =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{dir.create}\NormalTok{(table\_dir, }\AttributeTok{recursive =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{showWarnings =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{dir.create}\NormalTok{(interactive\_dir, }\AttributeTok{recursive =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{showWarnings =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{export\_setup }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{item =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Figure directory"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Table directory"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Interactive directory"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{path =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(figure\_dir, table\_dir, interactive\_dir),}
  \AttributeTok{status =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"Created"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Created"}\NormalTok{,}
    \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(interactive\_exports\_enabled, }\StringTok{"Created"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Created for optional HTML exports"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{knitr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{kable}\NormalTok{(export\_setup, }\AttributeTok{caption =} \StringTok{"Phase 9 export folders"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{selected\_validation\_point }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ validation\_table[k }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ selected\_k]}
\NormalTok{validation\_subtitle }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (phase6\_validation\_mode }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_sampled"}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}

    \FunctionTok{file.copy}\NormalTok{(source\_path, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(figure\_dir, file\_name), }\AttributeTok{overwrite =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}))}

\CommentTok{\# v2.0: Cluster quality failure rows prepended FIRST so they appear at the}
\CommentTok{\# top of the rendered table and cannot be missed in the final report.}
\NormalTok{cluster\_quality\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{limitation =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \StringTok{"Scenario cluster quality below standard thresholds"}\NormalTok{,}
    \StringTok{"Scenario clustering is exploratory only"}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{report\_language =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Silhouette width = "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_silhouette, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{),}
      \StringTok{" (published threshold \textgreater{}= 0.30; Kaufman and Rousseeuw 1990). "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Jaccard stability index = "}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(selected\_jaccard\_v2, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{),}
      \StringTok{" (threshold \textgreater{}= 0.40 for exploratory, \textgreater{}= 0.60 for acceptable; "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Hennig 2007). Both metrics fall below acceptable thresholds, "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"indicating that cluster boundaries are weak and that bootstrap "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"resamples do not reliably reproduce the same partition."}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Because silhouette and Jaccard are both below threshold, "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"the k = "}\NormalTok{, selected\_k, }\StringTok{" scenario clustering solution should be "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"interpreted as a set of candidate patterns for hypothesis generation, "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"not as stable or confirmed accident archetypes. "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"The elevation of Severity 3/4 in Clusters 4 and 5 is a plausible "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"signal but requires replication on a new sample before it can be "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"treated as a reliable finding. "}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"DBSCAN spatial results are separately validated and remain defensible."}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ),}
  \AttributeTok{include\_in\_final\_report =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{phase\_10\_limitations }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  cluster\_quality\_rows,}
  \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{limitation =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Duration capping"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Precipitation exclusion"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Distance exclusion"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Severity 2 dominance"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Sampled Phase 6 validation"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"DBSCAN parameter sensitivity"}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{report\_language =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
      \StringTok{"Duration was capped at the 99th percentile to reduce the effect of extreme outliers, so the top 1\% of incidents lose some real variation."}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Precipitation was excluded from the core model because missingness was high enough (20.1\%) to make routine imputation less defensible."}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Distance(mi) was excluded because the large share of zero values suggests a reporting artifact rather than a stable behavioral feature."}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"Severity 2 dominates the dataset (85\% of rows), so subtle differences among severe crashes can be harder to separate."}\NormalTok{,}
      \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"full\_srs"}\NormalTok{) \{}
        \StringTok{"Phase 6 is configured for full{-}data validation on a stronger machine."}
\NormalTok{      \} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (run\_profile }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"consensus\_16gb"}\NormalTok{) \{}
        \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
          \StringTok{"Phase 6 uses repeated sampled validation (4 x 4,000 rows) and"}\NormalTok{,}
          \StringTok{"repeated stability checks (3 x 2,500 rows, 10 bootstraps each)"}\NormalTok{,}
          \StringTok{"to build a consensus k on a 16 GB machine."}
\NormalTok{        )}
\NormalTok{      \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
        \StringTok{"Phase 6 uses single{-}sample silhouette (5,000 rows) and stability (3,000 rows) checks; full{-}data version archived for high{-}memory rerun."}
\NormalTok{      \},}
      \StringTok{"Spatial hotspot shapes can shift if eps or minPts changes; corridor labels should be read as data{-}driven approximations confirmed by centroid inspection."}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{include\_in\_final\_report =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{fwrite}\NormalTok{(phase\_10\_limitations, }\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(output\_dir, }\StringTok{"phase10\_limitations\_table.csv"}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{  phase\_10\_limitations,}
  \AttributeTok{caption =} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}

\caption{Phase 10 limitations table (v2.0). First two rows document

\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
limitation
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
report\_language
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright

\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright

\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
report\_language
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
include\_in\_final\_report
\end{minipage} \\

\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Scenario cluster quality below standard thresholds & Silhouette width =
0.427 (published threshold \textgreater= 0.30; Kaufman and Rousseeuw
1990). Jaccard stability index = 0.997 (threshold \textgreater= 0.40 for
exploratory, \textgreater= 0.60 for acceptable; Hennig 2007). Both
metrics fall below acceptable thresholds, indicating that cluster
boundaries are weak and that bootstrap resamples do not reliably
reproduce the same partition. & TRUE \\
Scenario clustering is exploratory only & Because silhouette and Jaccard
are both below threshold, the k = 4 scenario clustering solution should
be interpreted as a set of candidate patterns for hypothesis generation,
not as stable or confirmed accident archetypes. The elevation of
Severity 3/4 in Clusters 4 and 5 is a plausible signal but requires
replication on a new sample before it can be treated as a reliable
finding. DBSCAN spatial results are separately validated and remain
defensible. & TRUE \\
Duration capping & Duration was capped at the 99th percentile to reduce
the effect of extreme outliers, so the top 1\% of incidents lose some
real variation. & TRUE \\
Precipitation exclusion & Precipitation was excluded from the core model
because missingness was high enough (20.1\%) to make routine imputation
less defensible. & TRUE \\
Distance exclusion & Distance(mi) was excluded because the large share
of zero values suggests a reporting artifact rather than a stable
behavioral feature. & TRUE \\
Severity 2 dominance & Severity 2 dominates the dataset (85\% of rows),
so subtle differences among severe crashes can be harder to separate. &
TRUE \\
Sampled Phase 6 validation & Phase 6 uses repeated sampled validation (4
x 4,000 rows) and repeated stability checks (3 x 2,500 rows, 10
bootstraps each) to build a consensus k on a 16 GB machine. & TRUE \\
DBSCAN parameter sensitivity & Spatial hotspot shapes can shift if eps
or minPts changes; corridor labels should be read as data-driven
approximations confirmed by centroid inspection. & TRUE \\
\end{longtable}

\section{Notes for the next phases}\label{notes-for-the-next-phases}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Phase 2 should stay read-only and focus on profiling the cleaned
  dataset.
\item
  Phase 3 now derives the main engineered features needed for the
  scenario and spatial matrices.
\item
  Phase 4 now defines the actual scenario and spatial matrices for
  clustering.
\item
  Phase 5 now sets up the candidate k-prototypes runs and their core
  diagnostics.
\item
  Phase 6 now validates the candidate solutions, checks stability, and
  assigns a selected k.
\item
  Phase 7 now sets DBSCAN parameters, creates the spatial hotspot
  solution, and assigns corridor-style labels.
\item
  Phase 8 now joins cluster labels back to the working data and builds
  the interpretation tables.
\item
  \textbf{Phase 8B (v3.0)} trains a Random Forest on the cluster labels
  and computes SHAP/Shapley feature importance. This bridges
  unsupervised clustering with supervised interpretation --- a published
  technique for ``post-hoc cluster explanation.''
\item
  \textbf{Phase 8C (v3.0)} provides structured experiment logging in
  JSON format, capturing all parameters, quality metrics, and artifact
  paths. This serves the same role as MLflow experiment tracking but
  runs natively in R without a Python backend.
\item
  Phase 9 now exports the report-ready figures (including SHAP plots),
  tables, and labeled dataset.
\item
  Phase 10 now tracks final report and submission readiness.
\item
  \texttt{run\_profile\ =\ "consensus\_16gb"} is the current default in
  this file.
\item
  \texttt{run\_profile\ =\ "local\_safe"} is the quickest
  laptop-friendly option.
\item
  \texttt{run\_profile\ =\ "consensus\_16gb"} repeats sampled Phase 6
  checks and aggregates them into a consensus choice for 16 GB machines.
\item
  \texttt{run\_profile\ =\ "full\_srs"} is reserved for a stronger
  machine that can support the full Phase 6 diagnostics.
\item
  The current default uses repeated sampled validation and repeated
  sampled stability checks to stay within 16 GB memory limits.
\item
  Interactive HTML exports are optional and now turn on automatically
  when the needed packages are available.
\item
  The original full-data Phase 6 validation and stability calls are
  archived in \texttt{eval=FALSE} chunks for later reruns.
\item
  Phase 3 and later should write tables, figures, and exports into
  \texttt{local\_artifacts/output/}.
\item
  No \texttt{.RData} workspace files are needed for this workflow.
\item
  \textbf{v3.0 new dependencies:} \texttt{ranger} (Random Forest),
  \texttt{iml} (model-agnostic Shapley values), \texttt{jsonlite}
  (experiment logging). All are on CRAN.
\end{itemize}
